## Domain Knowledge
**Domain**: nonlinear oscillator dynamics
**Analysis**: This task involves modeling the acceleration (dv_dt) of a nonlinear harmonic oscillator as a function of position, velocity, and time. The acceleration is determined by restoring forces (functions of x) and damping forces (functions of v), potentially with nonlinear terms like cubic restoring forces (Duffing oscillator) or nonlinear damping.

**Common formula structures** (built-in generic + LLM domain-specific):
- Arrhenius equation: k = c0 * exp(c1 / T) (chemical reaction rate dependence on temperature)
- Coulomb's / Newton's inverse-square law: F = c0 / r**2 (gravitational or electrostatic force)
- Stefan-Boltzmann law: P = c0 * T**4 (blackbody radiation power vs temperature)
- Beer-Lambert law: I = c0 * exp(c1 * x) (light intensity attenuation through a medium)
- Michaelis-Menten kinetics: v = c0 * S / (S + c1) (enzyme-catalyzed reaction saturation)
- Hill equation: y = c0 * x**c1 / (x**c1 + c2) (cooperative binding, sigmoidal dose-response)
- Kepler's third law: T**2 = c0 * a**3 (orbital period vs semi-major axis)
- Newton's law of cooling: T = c0 + c1 * exp(c2 * t) (exponential thermal relaxation)
- Clausius-Clapeyron relation: log(P) = c0 + c1 / T (vapor pressure vs temperature)
- Langmuir adsorption isotherm: theta = c0 * P / (1 + c1 * P) (surface adsorption equilibrium)
- Freundlich isotherm: q = c0 * C**c1 (empirical adsorption on heterogeneous surface)
- Stokes' drag: F = c0 * r * v (viscous drag force on a sphere in fluid)
- Logistic growth: N = c0 / (1 + c1 * exp(c2 * t)) (population dynamics with carrying capacity)
- Planck-Wien approximation: I = c0 * f**3 * exp(c1 * f / T) (thermal radiation spectrum)
- Simple harmonic oscillator: dv_dt = c0 * x (linear restoring force)
- Damped harmonic oscillator: dv_dt = c0 * x + c1 * v (linear restoring + linear damping)
- Duffing oscillator: dv_dt = c0 * x + c1 * x**3 (cubic nonlinear restoring force)
- Damped Duffing oscillator: dv_dt = c0 * x + c1 * x**3 + c2 * v (cubic restoring + damping)
- Van der Pol oscillator: dv_dt = c0 * x + c1 * (1 - c2 * x**2) * v (nonlinear damping)
- Quintic nonlinear oscillator: dv_dt = c0 * x + c1 * x**3 + c2 * x**5 (higher-order restoring force)
- Nonlinear damping: dv_dt = c0 * x + c1 * v * abs(v) (quadratic velocity damping)
- Cubic damping: dv_dt = c0 * x + c1 * v**3 + c2 * x (nonlinear velocity-dependent dissipation)
- Forced Duffing: dv_dt = c0 * x + c1 * x**3 + c2 * v + c3 * cos(c4 * t) (periodically driven nonlinear oscillator)
- Softening spring: dv_dt = c0 * x * (1 + c1 * x**2) (position-dependent stiffness)
- Parametric oscillator: dv_dt = c0 * x * (1 + c1 * cos(c2 * t)) (time-varying stiffness)
- Mixed nonlinear: dv_dt = c0 * x + c1 * x**2 + c2 * x**3 (asymmetric restoring force with quadratic and cubic terms)
- Position-velocity coupling: dv_dt = c0 * x + c1 * x * v + c2 * v (cross-coupling between position and velocity)
- Rayleigh oscillator: dv_dt = c0 * x + c1 * v + c2 * v**3 (cubic velocity nonlinearity)

**Formula structure heuristic features**:
- Oscillation damping envelope ŌåÆ Exponential decay envelope f(x)*exp(-c*Abs(x)) for symmetric damped oscillation, Gaussian envelope f(x)*exp(-c*x**2) for localized wave packets
- Saturation/clipping effects ŌåÆ Rational fraction x/(1+x), tanh; for variables with alternating positive/negative in oscillatory systems, selectively apply Abs
- Growth/decay ŌåÆ Exponential growth exp(c*t), Logistic 1/(1+exp(-c*x)), power law x**c
- Threshold/activation behavior ŌåÆ Max(x-c, 0), piecewise functions
- Coupling/cross effects ŌåÆ Product terms between variables x*y, power-law coupling x**c1 * y**c2
- Odd-power restoring forces (x, x**3, x**5) ŌåÆ symmetric potential well / symmetric oscillation about equilibrium
- Even-power restoring terms (x**2) ŌåÆ asymmetric potential well / broken symmetry in oscillation
- Velocity-dependent terms proportional to v ŌåÆ linear energy dissipation or injection (linear damping/driving)
- Terms like (1 - x**2)*v ŌåÆ amplitude-dependent damping, self-sustained oscillations (limit cycles)
- Cubic position terms (x**3) with same/opposite sign as linear term ŌåÆ hardening/softening spring behavior
- Sinusoidal time-dependent terms cos(c*t) ŌåÆ external periodic forcing
- Products x*v ŌåÆ phase-space coupling, non-conservative forces that depend on both position and velocity
- Odd functions of v (v, v**3) ŌåÆ dissipation symmetric under time reversal of velocity sign

I need to compare each candidate against the Ground Truth (GT):

**GT:** `-1.02670587028003*x**3 - 1.02670587028003*x*exp(-Abs(x)) + 0.947981592038046*sin(t) - 0.712276797350088*sin(v)`

The GT has these basis functions:
1. `sin(t)` - with coefficient ~0.948
2. `sin(v)` - with coefficient ~-0.712
3. `x**3` - with coefficient ~-1.027
4. `x*exp(-Abs(x))` - with coefficient ~-1.027

Key observations:
- The GT contains `sin(v)`, not `v`, `v*Abs(v)`, or `v**3`
- The GT contains `x*exp(-Abs(x))`, which is a very specific function
- No candidate can match unless it can reproduce both `sin(v)` and `x*exp(-Abs(x))`

Let me check each candidate systematically:

**Candidates with `v` (linear), `v**3`, `v*Abs(v)` instead of `sin(v)`:**
These cannot match because `sin(v)` is not equivalent to any polynomial/piecewise polynomial in `v`. This eliminates candidates: 1, 2, 3, 4, 5, 8, 10, 15, 18, 19, 20, 21, 22, 23, 24, 25, 28, 29, 33, 34, 35, 36, 40, 41, 43, 44, 46, 50, 51, 52, 53, 54, 55, 56, 57, 58, 60, 61, 62, 63, 66.

**Candidates with `sin(c*v)` or `sin(c*v + c)`:**
- 6: `c0*sin(c1*t+c2) + c3*sin(c4*x+c5) + c6*v + c7*v**3 - x**3` ŌĆö Has `sin(c4*x+c5)` but needs `x*exp(-Abs(x))`, and has `v`, `v**3` instead of `sin(v)`. NO MATCH.
- 7: Has `sin(c4*v+c5)` (good for sin(v)) and `sin(c2*x)` but needs `x*exp(-Abs(x))`. sin(cx) ŌēĀ x*exp(-Abs(x)). NO MATCH.
- 13: `sin(c4*(c5*x+c6*v)+c7)` mixes x and v. Cannot separate into sin(v) + x*exp(-Abs(x)). NO MATCH.
- 14: Has `sin(c3*v)` (good), but needs `x*exp(-Abs(x))` ŌĆö only has polynomial terms in x. NO MATCH.
- 17: `sin(c2*v)` (good), but only `c3*x + c4*x**3` for x terms ŌĆö missing `x*exp(-Abs(x))`. NO MATCH.
- 27: `sin(c2*v)` (good), but only `c3*x + c4*x**3` ŌĆö missing `x*exp(-Abs(x))`. NO MATCH.
- 30: `sin(c2*v+c3)` (good), but only `c4*x + c5*x**3` ŌĆö missing `x*exp(-Abs(x))`. NO MATCH.
- 64: Has `sin(c2*x+c3)` and `log(c6*v+1)` ŌĆö log ŌēĀ sin. NO MATCH.

**Candidates with `sin(c*x)` terms:** These have `sin(cx)` trying to approximate `x*exp(-Abs(x))`. Since sin is periodic and `x*exp(-Abs(x))` is not, they cannot be equal. This eliminates: 9, 11, 37, 38, 39, 42, 45, 47, 48, 49, 65.

**Remaining:** 12, 16, 26, 31, 32, 59 ŌĆö these lack `sin(v)` entirely. NO MATCH.

Every candidate either lacks `sin(v)` (replacing it with polynomial/piecewise terms in v) or lacks `x*exp(-Abs(x))` (replacing it with sin, polynomial, or other non-equivalent functions).
